modules:\\n\\n**Offset Storage Layer (group-coordinator module):**\\nThe OffsetAndMetadata class represents the core offset storage, storing offset values with associated metadata like timestamps. The OffsetMetadataManager is the central handler for managing all offset operations - it implements the commitOffset() method (line 600) for processing OffsetCommitRequest and fetchOffsets() method (line 862) for handling OffsetFetchRequest. These methods manage the offset state stored in the __consumer_offsets topic.\\n\\n**Offset Expiry Mechanism:**\\nOffset expiration is controlled through the OffsetExpirationCondition interface and its implementation OffsetExpirationConditionImpl. These classes define when offsets should be considered expired based on configurable conditions, enabling automatic cleanup of stale offsets.\\n\\n**GroupCoordinator Implementation:**\\nThe GroupCoordinator class serves as the main interface for the group coordination service, handling all group-related requests including offset commits and fetches. GroupCoordinatorService provides the service layer, while GroupCoordinatorShard handles shard-level operations. GroupMetadataManager manages the complete group metadata including member information and offset data. GroupCoordinatorRecordHelpers and GroupCoordinatorRecordSerde handle serialization/deserialization of coordinator records for storage in __consumer_offsets.\\n\\n**Request Handling (core/server):**\\nThe KafkaApis.scala file contains the handleOffsetCommitRequest and handleOffsetFetchRequest methods that serve as the broker-side request handlers. These methods receive client requests and delegate to the GroupCoordinator for processing.\\n\\n**Coordinator State Persistence:**\\nCoordinatorPartitionWriter.scala writes coordinator records to the __consumer_offsets topic, persisting all offset commits and group state changes. CoordinatorLoaderImpl.scala loads the coordinator state from logs during broker startup, reconstructing the offset and group metadata from the __consumer_offsets topic.\\n\\n**Log Compaction for __consumer_offsets:**\\nThe LogCleaner, LogCleanerManager, and Cleaner classes in the storage module implement log compaction for the __consumer_offsets topic. These handle the cleanup and compaction of offset records, ensuring only the latest offset for each partition-consumer group combination is retained.\\n\\n**Client API Definitions:**\\nThe OffsetCommitRequest/Response and OffsetFetchRequest/Response classes define the wire protocol for offset operations.
